ups , including blood tests , while you are receiving treatment , especially at the start of treatment . this is to avoid postural hypotension ( a build - up of fluid in the body which carry the blood to form too low levels of red blood cells ). therefore , your doctor may decide to reduce the dose , interrupt , stop or change your treatment . you may also need other treatments . in some cases , it may be necessary to stop treatment with intravenous contraception . -
